[23-Aug-23 11:47 AM] exeler#0000
The list auctions command has some issues right now. It doesn't handle cases where there's a lot of auctions. 

So if there's too many auctions, discord rejects the message with all of them listed and the bot just shrugs and gives up. Then discord tells you the bot never responded, but it did try at least once.

[02-Feb-25 08:34 AM] evov#0000
I still have plenty of HE sitting at ANT (I raided the MOR CX and shipped it back to our CX). I just feel like the best course to correct a supply shortage is to ensure supply, but at a high price. It allows operations that 100% require that mat to continue, while providing a strong price signal to encourage increased production in the region.

Continuing to supply it at a typical price only pushes the production shortage issue down the road a couple weeks while also potentially causing critical issues for people that require that material.
